      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">八章五十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 30pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第一章总则、第二章重点专项概预算管理、第三章项目资金开支范围、第四章资项目预算编制与审批、第五章项目预算执行与调剂、第六章项目财务验收、第七章监督检查、第八章附则</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 15pt; mso-yfti-irow: 2">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 15pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第二条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 15pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">国家重点研发计划由若干目标明确、边界清晰的重点专项组成。重点专项下设项目，项目可根据自身特点和需要下设课题。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 30pt; mso-yfti-irow: 3">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 30pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第五条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 30pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">重点专项项目牵头承担单位、课题承担单位和课题参与单位应当是在中国大陆境内注册、具有独立法人资格的科研院所、高等院校、企业等。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 15pt; mso-yfti-irow: 4">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 15pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    rowSpan=12 width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第十七条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 15pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">重点专项项目资金由直接费用和间接费用组成。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 15pt; mso-yfti-irow: 5">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 15pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">注：直接费用和间接费用的内容与“财科教</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">[2017]74</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">号”基本一致，以下为“国科发资</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">[2017]261</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">号”的内容：</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 44.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 6">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 44.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">1.</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">设备费：应对购置仪器设备重点予以说明，包括设备的主要性能指标、主要技术参数和用途，对项目（课题）研究的作用，购置单台套</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">50</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">万元（含）以上的仪器设备，还需重点说明购买的必要性和数量的合理性等。购置单台套</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">10</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">万元（含）以上的设备，需提供</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">3</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">家以上报价单。如果是独家代理或生产，可提供</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">1</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">家报价单，但应予以说明。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 27.75pt; mso-yfti-irow: 7">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 27.75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">2.</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">材料费：如某一品种材料预算合计达到</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">10</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">万元（含）以上的大宗原辅材料、贵重材料等，应详细说明其与项目（课题）任务的相关性、购买的必要性、数量的合理性等。其余辅助材料、低值易耗品可按类别简要说明。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 43.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 8">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 43.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">3.</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">测试化验加工费：单次或累计费用在</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">10</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">万元（含）以上的测试化验加工项目，应详细说明其与项目（课题）研究任务的相关性、必要性，以及次数、价格等测算依据，并详细说明承接测试化验加工业务的外单位（包括承担单位内部独立经济核算单位）所具备的资质或相应能力。 
      如承接方与承担单位存在利益关联关系，应披露双方利益关联情况。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 45pt; mso-yfti-irow: 9">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 45pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">4.</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">编制燃料动力费：应按照相关仪器、科学装置等预计运行时间和所消耗的水、电、气、燃料等即期（预算编报时）价格测算，在测算过程中还应提供各参数来源或分摊依据、测算方法等。承担单位的日常水、电、气、暖消耗等费用不应在此科目编列，应在间接费用中解决。与项目（课题）研究任务相关的科学考察、野外实验勘探等发生的车、船、航空器的燃油费用可在燃料动力费中编列。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 60pt; mso-yfti-irow: 10">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 60pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">5.</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">出版</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">/</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">文献</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">/</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">信息传播</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">/</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">知识产权事务费：购买单价在</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">10</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">万元（含）以上的专用软件，应说明专用软件的主要技术指标和用途，购买的必要性和数量的合理性等，并需提供</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">3</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">家以上报价单。如果专用软件为独家代理或生产，可提供</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">1</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">家报价单，但应予以说明。中央财政资金中不应编列通用性操作系统、办公软件等非专用软件的购置费，以及日常手机和办公固定电话的通讯费、日常办公网络费和电话充值卡费用等。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 30pt; mso-yfti-irow: 11">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 30pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">6.</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">会议</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">/</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">差旅</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">/</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">国际合作交流费：会议次数、天数、人数以及会议费开支范围、标准等，中央高校、科研院所应按照其内部制定的管理办法测算，并提供管理办法作为附件。除中央高校、科研院所外，其他单位应参照国家关于会议费的相关开支标准进行测算。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 45pt; mso-yfti-irow: 12">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 45pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">7.</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">劳务费：承担单位为事业单位的，在编人员不得编列劳务费；承担单位为企业的，除为项目（课题）实施专门聘用的人员外，其他人员不得编列劳务费。上述人员可在项目（课题）间接费用的绩效支出中列支。劳务费的发放应符合本单位统一的薪酬体系规定，不得重复发放。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 30pt; mso-yfti-irow: 13">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 30pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">8.</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">专家咨询费：专家咨询费的发放应当按照国家有关规定由单位代扣代缴个人所得税（可将代扣代缴的个人所得税编列在内）。专家咨询费不得支付给参与项目（课题）研究及其管理的相关人员。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 15pt; mso-yfti-irow: 14">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 15pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">9.</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">其他支出：不得列支财务咨询业务发生的费用。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 30pt; mso-yfti-irow: 15">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 30pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">10.</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">间接费用：单位在申报间接费用预算时，应统筹安排，处理好分摊间接成本和对科研人员激励的关系。绩效支出安排应当与科研人员在项目工作中的实际贡献挂钩，绩效支出在间接费用中无比例限制。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 32.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 16">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 32.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第二十四条 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 32.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">项目申报单位应当按照政策相符性、目标相关性和经济合理性原则，科学、合理、真实地编制预算，对仪器设备购置、参与单位资质及拟外拨资金进行重点说明。项目申报单位对直接费用各项支出不得简单按比例编列。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 29.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 17">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 29.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    rowSpan=2 width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第二十八条 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 29.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">专业机构根据财政部下达的重点专项预算和科技部对项目安排建议的审核意见，向项目牵头承担单位下达重点专项项目预算，并与项目牵头承担单位签订项目任务书（含预算）。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 38.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 18">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 38.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">项目任务书（含预算）是项目和课题预算执行、财务验收和监督检查的依据。项目任务书（含预算）应以项目预算申报书为基础，突出绩效管理，明确项目考核目标、考核指标及考核方法，明晰各方责权，明确课题承担单位和参与单位的资金额度，包括其他来源资金和其他配套条件等。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 27.75pt; mso-yfti-irow: 19">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 27.75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    rowSpan=2 width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第二十九条 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 27.75pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">专业机构应当按照国库集中支付制度规定</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">,</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">及时办理向项目牵头承担单位支付年度项目资金的有关手续。实行部门预算批复前项目资金预拨制度。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 28.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 20">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 28.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">项目牵头承担单位应当根据课题研究进度和资金使用情况，及时向课题承担单位拨付资金。课题承担单位应当按照研究进度，及时向课题参与单位拨付资金。课题参与单位不得再向外转拨资金。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-fareast-language: EN-US">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 27pt; mso-yfti-irow: 21">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 27pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第三十条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 27pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">承担单位应当严格执行国家有关财经法规和财务制度，切实履行法人责任，建立健全项目资金内部管理制度和报销规定，明确内部管理权限和审批程序，完善内控机制建设，强化资金使用绩效评价，确保资金使用安全规范有效。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 19.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 22">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 19.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第三十一条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"> 
      </SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 19.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">承担单位应当建立健全科研财务助理制度，为科研人员在项目预算编制和调剂、资金支出、财务决算和验收方面提供专业化服务。</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 29.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 23">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 29.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第三十二条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 29.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">承担单位应当将项目资金纳入单位财务统一管理，对中央财政资金和其他来源的资金分别单独核算，确保专款专用。按照承诺保证其他来源的资金及时足额到位。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 31.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 24">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 31.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第三十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 31.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">承担单位应当建立信息公开制度，在单位内部公开项目立项、主要研究人员、资金使用（重点是间接费用、外拨资金、结余资金使用等）、大型仪器设备购置以及项目研究成果等情况，接受内部监督。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 27pt; mso-yfti-irow: 25">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 27pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    rowSpan=4 width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第三十六条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 27pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">承担单位应当按照下达的预算执行。项目在研期间，年度剩余资金结转下一年度继续使用。预算确有必要调剂时，应当按照以下调剂范围和权限，履行相关程序：</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 27pt; mso-yfti-irow: 26">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 27pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">（一）项目预算总额调剂，项目预算总额不变、课题间预算调剂，课题预算总额不变、课题参与单位之间预算调剂以及增减参与单位的，由项目牵头承担单位或课题承担单位逐级向专业机构提出申请，专业机构审核评估后，按有关规定批准。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 51pt; mso-yfti-irow: 27">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 51pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">（二）课题预算总额不变，课题直接费用中材料费、测试化验加工费、燃料动力费、出版</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">/</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">文献</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">/</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">信息传播</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">/</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">知识产权事务费、其他支出预算如需调剂，课题负责人根据实施过程中科研活动的实际需要提出申请，由课题承担单位批准，报项目牵头承担单位备案。设备费、差旅</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">/</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">会议</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">/</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">国际合作交流费、劳务费、专家咨询费的预算一般不予调增，需调减用于课题其他直接支出的，可按上述程序办理调剂审批手续；如有特殊情况确需调增的，由项目（课题）负责人提出申请，经项目牵头承担单位同意后，报专业机构批准。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 18pt; mso-yfti-irow: 28">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 18pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">（三）课题间接费用预算总额不得调增，经课题承担单位与课题负责人协商一致后，可以调减用于直接费用。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 26.25pt; mso-yfti-irow: 29">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 26.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第四十条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 26.25pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">项目执行期满后，项目牵头承担单位应当及时组织课题承担单位清理账目与资产，如实编制课题资金决算。项目牵头承担单位审核汇总后向专业机构提出财务验收申请。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR>
  <TR style="HEIGHT: 31.5pt; mso-yfti-irow: 30; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 31.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 9.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.9pt; BORDER-LEFT: black 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="9%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt" 
      align=center><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">第四十二条</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 31.5pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 90.5%; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0.5pt; PADDING-TOP: 0.25pt; PADDING-LEFT: 5.65pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.9pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent" 
    width="90%">
      <P class=pMsoNormal style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt"><FONT face=Calibri><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN">财务验收应当按项目组织，以项目下设的课题为单元开展和出具财务验收结论，综合形成项目财务验收意见，并告知项目牵头承担单位。</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; mso-bidi-language: #0400">&nbsp;</SPAN><SPAN 
      style="mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN"><FONT 
      size=3>&nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P></TD></TR></TBODY></TABLE></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<B>（三）国家自然科学基金资助项目和国家社会科学基金项目</B> <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
1.国家自然科学基金资助项目 <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
国家自然科学基金资助项目，是指按照《国家自然科学基金条例》规定，用于资助科学技术人员开展基础研究和科学前沿探索，支持人才和团队建设的专项资金。国家自然科学基金委员会依法负责项目的立项和审批，并对项目资金进行具体管理和监督。依托单位是项目资金管理的责任主体，项目负责人是项目资金使用的直接责任人，对资金使用的合规性、合理性、真实性和相关性承担法律责任。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
2015年4月，财政部、自然科学基金委发布《国家自然科学基金资助项目资金管理办法》（财教[2015]15号），对2002年6月发布的（财教[2002]65号）文进行重新修订。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
2.国家社会科学基金项目 <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
国家社会科学基金项目，是用于资助哲学社会科学研究，促进哲学社会科学学科发展、人才培养和队伍建设的专项资金。全国哲学社会科学规划领导小组领导国家社科基金管理工作。项目责任单位是项目资金管理的责任主体，负责项目资金的日常管理和监督。项目负责人是项目资金使用的直接责任人，对资金使用的合规性、合理性、真实性和相关性承担法律责任。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
2016年9月财政部、全国哲学社会科学规划领导小组发布了《国家社会科学基金项目经费管理办法》（财教[2007]30号），对2007年4月发布的（财教[2016]304号）文进行重新修订。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<H3 
style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: auto; MARGIN: 12pt 0cm 3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 15pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>三、财务验收关注事项<o:p></o:p></SPAN></H3>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
目前，民口科技重大专项的财务验收办法已经发布，重点研发计划项目的财务验收根据《国务院关于优化科研管理提升科研绩效若干措施的通知》（国发[2018]25号）的有关规定与技术验收合并进行。具体由项目管理专业机构严格依据任务书在项目实施期末进行一次性综合绩效评价，不再分别开展单独的财务验收和技术验收。根据《国家重点研发计划资金管理办法》的要求，科技部对财务审计和财务验收进行随机抽查。对财务审计，重点抽查审计依据充分性、结论可靠性、审计工作质量及对重大违规问题的披露情况。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
以重大专项为例，财务验收采取现场验收、非现场验收或两者相结合等方式。财务验收的内容主要有： <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<B>（一）财务管理及相关制度建设情况</B> <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
项目（课题）承担单位是否建立预算管理、资金管理、合同管理、政府采购、审批报销、资产管理和内部控制等制度；如项目（课题）涉及基本建设，则需制定基建管理制度；以及上述制度的内容是否合理等。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<B>（二）资金到位和拨付情况</B> <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
重大专项各渠道资金的到位情况，以及项目（课题）牵头承担单位是否按预算批复和合同任务书（含预算书，下同）对参与单位及时足额拨付资金等。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<B>（三）会计核算和财务支出情况</B> <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
项目（课题）承担单位的会计核算是否规范、准确、真实；项目（课题）的实际支出是否按照预算执行（包括调剂后的预算）；项目（课题）的实际支出是否符合有关规定的支出范围和支出标准；项目（课题）的支出与项目（课题）内容的相关性和合理性等。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
承担单位应当将项目资金纳入单位财务统一管理，对中央财政资金和其他来源的资金分别单独核算，确保专款专用。 <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<B>（四）预算执行情况</B> <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
项目（课题）的预算执行情况和项目（课题）的预算调剂是否按照规定程序和权限进行，以及各类资金结余情况等。 <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<B>（五）资产管理情况</B> <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
资产配置是否符合新增资产配置预算、政府采购及合同管理制度的规定，资产使用及处置是否符合资产管理制度情况，设备类资产的使用效率及开放共享情况；以及无形资产管理的情况等。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<H3 
style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: auto; MARGIN: 12pt 0cm 3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 15pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>四、其他事项<o:p></o:p></SPAN></H3>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
2018年7月，国务院下发《关于优化科研管理提升科研绩效若干措施的通知》，要求优化科研项目和经费管理、完善有利于创新的评价激励制度，以及开展基于绩效、诚信和能力的科研管理改革试点。按照能放尽放的要求，赋予科研人员更大的人财物自主支配权，简化科研项目申报和过程管理、合并财务验收和技术验收、直接费用中除设备费外的其他科目费用调剂权全部下放给项目承担单位等。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
针对通知的相关要求，现行的相关规定尚未修订。在此，提示会计师事务所和注册会计师关注政策的后续变化情况，及时更新相关审计流程和审计工作底稿。 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 26pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 13pt; FONT-FAMILY: "微软雅黑",sans-serif; mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-bidi-font-family: 微软雅黑'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style='mso-bidi-language: #0400; mso-ansi-language: ZH-CN; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; mso-margin-top-alt: auto; mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT size=3 
face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
